                  </form> act. part. n. of 1 [signifying <hi rend="ital">Absent; distant,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">remote;</hi> and <hi rend="ital">hidden, concealed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">unapparent;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">absent from the range,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">beyond the reach, of perception by sense,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">of mental perception</hi>]: pl. (applied to men, K, TA) <foreign lang="ar">غُيَّبٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">غُيَّابٌ</foreign> (S, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">غَائِبُونَ</foreign> (K) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n32693-1" target="غَيَبٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n32685"/></foreign>, (S, Mgh, K,) or rather the last is a quasi-pl. n., (TA,) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n32693-2" target="غَيْبٌ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n32684"/></foreign>, [which is also properly speaking a quasi-pl. n.,] like <foreign lang="ar">صَحْبٌ</foreign>: (Msb [in which <foreign lang="ar">غَيَبٌ</foreign> is not mentioned]:) the <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> in   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n32693-3" target="غَيَبٌ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n32685"/></foreign> remains unchanged, notwithstanding the two fet-hahs, because it is likened to <foreign lang="ar">صَيَدٌ</foreign>, and, although it is a pl. [in signification] and <foreign lang="ar">صَيَدٌ</foreign> is an inf. n., it may be used as meant for an inf. n. (S, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  See also <foreign lang="ar">غَيْبٌ</foreign>, first sentence.          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">A run in which a horse reserves</hi> [<hi rend="ital">somewhat of his force for the time of need</hi>]. (A in art. <foreign lang="ar">شهد</foreign>: see <foreign lang="ar">شَاهِدٌ</foreign>.)
